# Per-Test-Case Performance Grids (P / R / F1)

Each cell is precision / recall / F1. Rows = prompt complexity, columns = evaluation tier. Cells since 20260516T000000Z, non-empty-wins dedup (reconciles with the headline sweep report). '—' = no scored cell.

- **naive** = untrained-user phrasing · **broad** = clinically-aware, no codes · **expert** = code-aware spec
- **T1** = closed-book · **T2** = agentic+tools · **T3** = +methodology

## All-up F1 leaderboard (comprehensive / all-patients cell)

Mean F1 over each phenotype's **all-patients** test case (`-comprehensive` where it exists, else the base case), averaged across the naive/broad/expert prompts. This is the high-level model comparison: *how well does each model find the whole cohort?*

| model | T1 closed-book | T2 agentic+tools | T3 +methodology |
|-------|----|----|----|
| `copilot:claude-sonnet-4.6` | **0.760** (97%) | **0.917** (97%) | **0.896** (97%) |
| `copilot:gpt-5.4` | **0.704** (100%) | **0.913** (95%) | **0.906** (96%) |
| `openai-compat:qwen-qwen3.5-9b` | **0.294** (99%) | **0.533** (99%) | **0.778** (100%) |

(Percentages = canonical-cell coverage; means are over scored cells.)

## Coverage

Share of cells with a scored result ('—' cells are unscored: timeout, agentic error, or only run before the cutoff window).

| model | T1 | T2 | T3 |
